name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted March 25, 2024
msg:The hotel is in a suitable location, very close to the highway, convenient for self-driving, and about 10 minutes' drive from Baishi Mountain Scenic Area.
I stayed in late March, so there were not many people on weekends. The Japanese-style hot spring room was quiet and clean, and my children loved it. Compared with indoor and outdoor hot springs, the private hot spring pool is quite large and the water temperature is easy to adjust, but there are no programs on the TV.
The overall service is warm and welcoming. I would like to give a special thumbs up to Wang Xiaofen, the housekeeper who received us. He proactively provided fruits, contacted the shuttle bus, and asked the children about their stay and play experience. It felt very warm.
The breakfast was better than expected. The animals in the Qingqing Ranch that comes with the package are in good condition. The free-range ducks and geese are very enthusiastic and suitable for parents and children.
The degree of development of Baishi Mountain is average. It has fewer people, good scenery, and convenient ropeway rides. You can consider coming here to escape the heat in summer.

The hotel also provided a fruit plate as a gift. It was quite comfortable to eat fruit while taking a bath!
The breakfast is quite satisfactory, with mostly Chinese and less Western options. Itâ€™s enough to enjoy!
Need to explain: Currently, only some indoor and outdoor hot springs in the facility are open. The tropical rainforest hot springs, children's water park and swimming pool are not open due to renovation! In order to experience various hot spring baths and play with children, please pay attention in advance. Before going, you can call in advance to ask whether the hotel has been renovated! Otherwise, it will be in vain and it will affect the experience!
